402. Commit: d13b7b80
   SHA: d13b7b80d1240cb4f079743d3778723d5dbf9b35
   Message: refactor: Refactored the uploadFile method (#1066)

* refactor: Refactored the uploadFile method

Refactored the uploadFile method. In the previous step, when applying for a document upload lease, the HTTP request parameters returned for uploading the document may have a Content-Type that is null. However, the server requires that the empty Content-Type be preserved during the upload. When using RestTemplate, if Content-Type is null, it gets removed automatically, causing the request to be incorrect. Therefore, the implementation has been updated to use OkHttp for the upload, ensuring that the Content-Type field, even if empty, remains in the request.

* fix(ci): PR title labeler renamed

PR title labeler renamed, changed reactor to refactor.

* chore(core): add unit tests for uploadFile

* style(core): format the code

1.replace the fake data in the mock Excel file with Chinese characters
2.format the code

* style(core): Update the mock request header values in the test cases.

* style(core): format the code

* style(core): format the code

* chore(core): format the unit test code
